    cookieUsuario[7] = "";

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function async(callback) {
    setTimeout(callback, 0);
  }

  function createDeferElement(theNode) {
    var newNode = document.createElement(theNode.tagName);
    if (newNode.tagName == 'SCRIPT') {
      //newNode.async = theNode.getAttribute('async') != null;
      if (theNode.getAttribute('defer-src') != null) {
        newNode.src = theNode.getAttribute('defer-src');
      } else {
        newNode.innerHTML = theNode.innerHTML;
      }
    } else {
      if (theNode.getAttribute('defer-href') != null) {
        newNode.href = theNode.getAttribute('defer-href');
        newNode.setAttribute('rel', 'stylesheet');
      }
    }
    newNode.type = theNode.getAttribute('type').replace('/defer', '');
    return newNode;
  }

  
  /*Home*/
  /*! loadCSS. [c]2017 Filament Group, Inc. MIT License */
  /* This file is meant as a standalone workflow for
  - testing support for link[rel=preload]
  - enabling async CSS loading in browsers that do not support rel=preload
  - applying rel preload css once loaded, whether supported or not.
  */
  (function(w) {
    "use strict";
    // rel=preload support test
    if (!w.loadCSS) {
      w.loadCSS = function() {};
    }
    // define on the loadCSS obj
    var rp = loadCSS.relpreload = {};
    // rel=preload feature support test
    // runs once and returns a function for compat purposes
    rp.support = (function() {
      var ret;
      try {
        ret = w.document.createElement("link").relList.supports("preload");
      } catch (e) {
        ret = false;
      }
      return function() {
        return ret;
      };
    })();
    // if preload isn't supported, get an asynchronous load by using a non-matching media attribute
    // then change that media back to its intended value on load
    rp.bindMediaToggle = function(link) {
      // remember existing media attr for ultimate state, or default to 'all'
      var finalMedia = link.media || "all";

      function enableStylesheet() {
        link.media = finalMedia;
      }
      // bind load handlers to enable media
      if (link.addEventListener) {
        link.addEventListener("load", enableStylesheet);
      } else if (link.attachEvent) {
        link.attachEvent("onload", enableStylesheet);
      }
      // Set rel and non-applicable media type to start an async request
      // note: timeout allows this to happen async to let rendering continue in IE
      setTimeout(function() {
        link.rel = "stylesheet";
        link.media = "only x";
      });
      // also enable media after 3 seconds,
      // which will catch very old browsers (android 2.x, old firefox) that don't support onload on link
      setTimeout(enableStylesheet, 3000);
    };
    // loop through link elements in DOM
    rp.poly = function() {
      // double check this to prevent external calls from running
      if (rp.support()) {
        return;
      }
      var links = w.document.getElementsByTagName("link");
      for (var i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
        var link = links[i];
        // qualify links to those with rel=preload and as=style attrs
        if (link.rel === "preload" && link.getAttribute("as") === "style" && !link.getAttribute("data-loadcss")) {
          // prevent rerunning on link
          link.setAttribute("data-loadcss", true);
          // bind listeners to toggle media back
          rp.bindMediaToggle(link);
        }
      }
    };
    // if unsupported, run the polyfill
    if (!rp.support()) {
      // run once at least
      rp.poly();
      // rerun poly on an interval until onload
      var run = w.setInterval(rp.poly, 500);
      if (w.addEventListener) {
        w.addEventListener("load", function() {
          rp.poly();
          w.clearInterval(run);
        });
      } else if (w.attachEvent) {
        w.attachEvent("onload", function() {
          rp.poly();
          w.clearInterval(run);
        });
      }
    }
    // commonjs
    if (typeof exports !== "undefined") {
      exports.loadCSS = loadCSS;
    } else {
      w.loadCSS = loadCSS;
    }
    var loadJS = function(src, cb) {
      "use strict";
      var ref = w.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
      var script = w.document.createElement("script");
      script.src = src;
      script.async = true;
      ref.parentNode.insertBefore(script, ref);
      if (cb && typeof(cb) === "function") {
        script.onload = cb;
      }
      return script;
    };
    // commonjs
    if (typeof module !== "undefined") {
      module.exports = loadJS;
    } else {
      w.loadJS = loadJS;
    }
  }(typeof global !== "undefined" ? global : this));

  
    /*Home*/
    function dCSS() {
      var cssobjs = document.querySelectorAll('link[as="style"]');
      for (var i = 0; i < cssobjs.length; i++) {
      cssobjs[i].rel = 'stylesheet';
      }
    }

  

  function dTPJS() {
    var objs = document.querySelectorAll('script[type="text/javascript/defer"]'),
      inlineScript = '';
    for (var i = 0; i < objs.length; i++) {
      if (objs[i].getAttribute('defer-src') != null) {
        var newNode = document.createElement(objs[i].tagName);
        newNode.src = objs[i].getAttribute('defer-src');
        newNode.type = objs[i].getAttribute('type').replace('/defer', '');
        objs[i].parentNode.insertBefore(createDeferElement(objs[i]), objs[i]);
        objs[i].parentNode.removeChild(objs[i]);
      } else {
        inlineScript += objs[i].innerHTML;
      }
    }
    if (inlineScript.length > 0) {
      var newNode = document.createElement('script');
      newNode.innerHTML = inlineScript;
      objs[objs.length - 1].parentNode.insertBefore(newNode, objs[objs.length - 1]);
    }
    return async(dIFR);
  }

  function dIFR() {
    var vidDefer = document.getElementsByTagName('iframe');
    for (var i = 0; i < vidDefer.length; i++) {
      if (vidDefer[i].getAttribute('data-src')) {
        vidDefer[i].setAttribute('src', vidDefer[i].getAttribute('data-src'));
      }
    }
    return;
  }

  function dLJS() {

    loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/lazysizes.min.js", function() {});
    loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/jquery.js", function() {
      loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/lazysizes-allloaded.min.js");
      
        loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/all.fn_home.js", function() {
      
          loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/i18n.js", function() {
            loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/cookie_realmadrid.js");
            loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/popups.js");
            loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/search_results.js");
            loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/calendar.js");
            loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/gallery_modificado.js");
            loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/cabecera_login_usuario.js");
            loadJS("/StaticFiles/RealMadridResponsive/javascripts/all.js", function() {
              RM._execute_callbacks('load');
              //async(dTPGPT);
              async(dTPJS);
            });
        });
      });
    });
  }

  function defer() {
    return window.isLoaded = true, dCSS(), dLJS();
  }
  if (window.addEventListener)
    window.addEventListener("load", defer, false);
  else if (window.attachEvent)
    window.attachEvent("onload", defer);
  else window.onload = defer;

   <script type="text/javascript/defer">
    // idioma de navegacion
  var idioma_ind = "castellano";

  var f = false,
      b = false,
      v = false,
      m = false,
      d = false, // ninguna
      w = true, // idioma
      litFutbolES = 'fútbol'.replace(new RegExp(/[ùúûü]/g),"u");
      litBaloncestoES = 'baloncesto';
      litVentajasES = 'ventajas';
      litMadridistasES = 'madridistas';
      litNingunaES = 'desactivar';
      litFutbol = 'Fútbol';
      litBaloncesto = 'Baloncesto';
      litVentajas = 'Ventajas';
      litMadridistas = 'Madridistas';
      litNinguna = 'Desactivar';
      canales = [litFutbolES, litBaloncestoES, litVentajasES, litMadridistasES, litNingunaES];
//canales = ['futbol', 'baloncesto', 'ventajas', 'madridistas', 'ninguna'];

  var removePopup = function() {
    var pop_p = document.getElementById('indiag');
    pop_p.outerHTML = '';
    return true;
  };

  var createInDialog = function() {

    // get de suscripciones actuales
    navigator.indigitall.getSubscriptions(function(tags){

      if(Array.isArray(tags) && tags.length > 0){
        tags.forEach(function(tag) {
          if (tag.tag_id == 'futbol') f = true;
          if (tag.tag_id == 'baloncesto') b = true;
          if (tag.tag_id == 'promociones') v = true;
          if (tag.tag_id == 'madridistas') m = true;
          if (tag.tag_id == 'desactivar') d = true;
        });
      }

      //Mostramos popup para configurar suscripciones
      createInDialogHTML();

    }, onIndigitallError);
  };

  var createInDialogHTML = function() {

    // popup
    var pop = document.createElement('div');
    pop.id = 'indiag';
    // cabecera
    var pop_h = document.createElement('h3');
    pop_h.className = 'notifhead';
    pop_h.innerHTML = "¡No te pierdas ninguna de nuestras notificaciones!";
    // Agrega cabecera a popup
    pop.appendChild(pop_h);
    // form
    var pop_f = document.createElement('form');
    pop_f.className = 'notiform';
    // fieldset
    var pop_s = document.createElement('fieldset');
    // legend
    var pop_l = document.createElement('legend');
    pop_l.className = 'notifleg';
    pop_l.innerHTML = "Selecciona las notificaciones que más te interesan:";
    // Agrega legend a fliedset
    pop_s.appendChild(pop_l);
    // inputs
    canales.forEach(function(canal) {
      // span
      var pop_n = document.createElement('span');
      // label
      var pop_a = document.createElement('label');
      pop_a.htmlFor = 'notif_' + canal.charAt(0).toLowerCase();
      pop_a.className = 'notiflabel';
      // input
      var pop_i = document.createElement('input');
      pop_i.type = 'checkbox';
      pop_i.id = 'notif_' + canal.charAt(0).toLowerCase();
      pop_i.value = canal.normalize('NFD').replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g, '').replace(/\s/g, '_').toLowerCase();
      if(canal.charAt(0).toLowerCase() == 'f') pop_i.checked = f;
      if(canal.charAt(0).toLowerCase() == 'b') pop_i.checked = b;
      if(canal.charAt(0).toLowerCase() == 'v') pop_i.checked = v;
      if(canal.charAt(0).toLowerCase() == 'm') pop_i.checked = m;
	    if(canal.charAt(0).toLowerCase() == 'd') pop_i.checked = d;
      // Evento checkboxes
      pop_i.addEventListener('click', function(e){
        var etv = e.target.value;
        var trg = Array.from(e.target.closest('fieldset').querySelectorAll('span .notiflabel .checkbox input'));

      if (etv == 'desactivar') {

        var chk = trg.filter(function (obj) {
          return obj.value != etv;
        });
        chk.forEach(function (el) {
          el.checked = false;
          el.closest('span.checkbox').classList.remove('checked_checkbox');
        });
        e.target.checked = true;
        e.target.closest('span.checkbox').classList.add('checked_checkbox');
        f = false, b = false, v = false, m = false, d = true;

      } else {

        var nin = trg.filter(function (obj) {
          return obj.value == 'desactivar';
        });

        var chk = trg.filter(function (obj) {
          return obj.checked == true;
        });

        f = false, b = false, v = false, m = false;
        chk.forEach(function (el) {
          if (el.id.slice(-1) == 'f') f = true;
          if (el.id.slice(-1) == 'b') b = true;
          if (el.id.slice(-1) == 'v') v = true;
          if (el.id.slice(-1) == 'm') m = true;
          if (el.id.slice(-1) == 'd') d= true;
        });

        if (nin[0].checked == true && chk.length > 0) {
          d = false;
          nin[0].checked = false;
          nin[0].closest('span.checkbox').classList.remove('checked_checkbox');
        } else if (nin[0].checked == false && chk.length == 0) {
          d = true;
          nin[0].checked = true;
          nin[0].closest('span.checkbox').classList.add('checked_checkbox');
        }

      }

    }); // Agrega input a label
      pop_a.appendChild(pop_i);
      // Texto canal
	  if (canal === litFutbolES){
		  var pop_c = document.createTextNode(litFutbol);
	  }else if (canal === litBaloncestoES){
		  var pop_c = document.createTextNode(litBaloncesto);
	  } else if (canal === litVentajasES){
		  var pop_c = document.createTextNode(litVentajas);
	  } else if (canal === litMadridistasES){
		  var pop_c = document.createTextNode(litMadridistas);
	  } else if (canal === litNingunaES){
		  var pop_c = document.createTextNode(litNinguna);
	  }
      // Agrega texto a label
      pop_a.appendChild(pop_c);
      // Agrega label a span
      pop_n.appendChild(pop_a);
      // Agrega span a fieldset
      pop_s.appendChild(pop_n);
    });
    // Agrega fieldset a form
    pop_f.appendChild(pop_s);
    // btn
    var pop_b = document.createElement('button');
    pop_b.name = 'button';
    pop_b.className = 'btn notifbut';
    pop_b.innerHTML = "Guardar";
    // Evento btn
    pop_b.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      subscribe(f, b, v, m, d, w);
      var pop_p = document.getElementById('indiag');
      pop_p.classList.remove('show');
      // quito popup
      window.setTimeout(removePopup, 550);
    });
    // Agrega botón a form
    pop_f.appendChild(pop_b);
    // Agrega form a popup
    pop.appendChild(pop_f);
    // nota
    var pop_t = document.createElement('p');
    pop_t.className = 'notifnote';
    pop_t.innerHTML = "Si en algún momento deseas cambiar las preferencias de tus notificaciones puedes hacerlo en el pie de la página.";
    // Agrega nota a popup
    pop.appendChild(pop_t);
    // Agrega popup a docuemnto
    document.body.appendChild(pop);
    // Custom checkboxes - Depende de jQuery y Custom-form
    var inputs = $(pop).find("[type=checkbox], [type=radio], select");
    inputs.custom_form();
    // Enseña popup
    pop.classList.toggle('show');
  };

  var subscribe = function(f, b, v, m, d, w) {
    var _subscribe = [];
    if (f) {
      _subscribe.push('futbol');
    }
    if (b) {
      _subscribe.push('baloncesto');
    }
    if (v) {
      _subscribe.push('promociones');
    }
    if (m) {
      _subscribe.push('madridistas');
    }
    if (d && !( f || b || v || m )) {
      navigator.indigitall.disable();
    }
    if (w) {
      _subscribe.push( idioma_ind );
    }


    //Reset de las suscripciones anteriores
    var tagIds = ["futbol", "baloncesto", "promociones", "madridistas","desactivar", idioma_ind];
    navigator.indigitall.unsubscribe(tagIds, function(){

      //Suscripción a las nuevas
      if (_subscribe.length > 0) {
        navigator.indigitall.subscribe(_subscribe, function(){

          //LOG
          //console.log("Suscripción a los tags: ", _subscribe);

        }, onIndigitallError);
      }
    }, onIndigitallError);
  };


  var idioma_temp = ""; // temporal para grupo de idioma

  var change_language = function() {

    // get de suscripciones actuales
    navigator.indigitall.getSubscriptions(function(tags){

      if(Array.isArray(tags) && tags.length > 0){
        tags.forEach(function(tag) {
        // console.log(" tag id --- " + tag.tag_id);
        if (tag.tag_id === 'castellano') idioma_temp = tag.tag_id;
        if (tag.tag_id === 'frances')    idioma_temp = tag.tag_id;
        if (tag.tag_id === 'portugues')   idioma_temp = tag.tag_id;
        if (tag.tag_id === 'indonesio')  idioma_temp = tag.tag_id;
        if (tag.tag_id === 'japones')    idioma_temp = tag.tag_id;
        if (tag.tag_id === 'arabe')      idioma_temp = tag.tag_id;
        if (tag.tag_id === 'ingles')     idioma_temp = tag.tag_id;
        if (tag.tag_id === 'aleman')     idioma_temp = tag.tag_id;
        if (tag.tag_id === 'hindi')      idioma_temp = tag.tag_id;
        });
      };


      //Reset de las suscripciones anteriores
      if ( idioma_temp !== "" ){
        // si no viene nada suscribimos
        subscribe_idioma(w);
      } else if ( ( idioma_temp !== "" ) && ( idioma_temp !== idioma_ind ) ) {
        // si el idioma que viene no coincide con el de navegacion suscribimos
        subscribe_idioma(w);
      }

    }, onIndigitallError);
  };

 var subscribe_idioma = function(w){

    var tag_idioma = [idioma_temp];

    if ( tag_idioma.length > 0 ){

    navigator.indigitall.unsubscribe(tag_idioma, function(){

      //console.log("nos quitamos del idioma " + tag_idioma);

      // nos subscribimos solo si no hay otro idioma
      var _subscribe_idioma = [];

      if (w) {
        _subscribe_idioma.push(idioma_ind);
      }

      //Suscripción a las nuevas
      if ( _subscribe_idioma.length > 0 ){
        navigator.indigitall.subscribe(_subscribe_idioma, function(){
          //LOG
          //console.log("Suscripción a los tags: ", _subscribe_idioma);
        }, onIndigitallError);
      }

    }, onIndigitallError);

	} else {
	
		  // nos subscribimos solo si no hay otro idioma
		  var _subscribe_idioma = [];

		  if (w) {
			_subscribe_idioma.push(idioma_ind);
		  }

		  //Suscripción a las nuevas
		  if ( _subscribe_idioma.length > 0 ){
			navigator.indigitall.subscribe(_subscribe_idioma, function(){
			  //LOG
			  //console.log("Suscripción a los tags: ", _subscribe_idioma);
			}, onIndigitallError);
		  }

	} // else

  }


  document.addEventListener('indigitallReady', function() {

    // admin event
    var not_adm = document.getElementById('notif_link');
    not_adm.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();

      // Verificar si las notificaciones están habilitadas
      if (Notification.permission !== "granted" && !document.getElementById('indiag')) {

        // Creamos tooltip
        not_adm.classList.toggle('notif_enable');
        // Para gestionar las notificaciones debe permitir las notificaciones en su navegador

      } else {

        // Crear dialogo
        if (!document.getElementById('indiag')) {
          createInDialog();
        }
      }
    });

    //Carga del SDK indigitall
    var prevPermission = Notification.permission;
    navigator.indigitall.loadIndigitall(function(){
      var newUser = (prevPermission !== "granted" && Notification.permission === "granted");

      //LOG
      //console.log("Nuevo usuario web push: ", newUser);

      if(newUser){
        createInDialog();
      }

      // si tenemos permisos registramos en el grupo del idioma correspondiente
      if( Notification.permission === "granted" ){

        //console.log(" entramos idioma indigitall >>> " + idioma_ind );
        change_language();

      }

    }, onIndigitallError);
  });

  function onIndigitallError(){
    console.error('Indigitall error:', arguments);
  }

  var scriptIndigitall = document.createElement('script');
      scriptIndigitall.type = 'text/javascript';
      scriptIndigitall.async = true;
      scriptIndigitall.src = 'https://www.realmadrid.com/indigitall/indigitall.min.js';
  document.body.appendChild(scriptIndigitall);
